LBDLDLM = (LBXTC-(LBDHDD + LBXTR/Adjustable Factor), round to 0 decimal places) for LBXTR less than 400 mg/dL, and missing for LBXTR greater than 400 mg/dL. LBDLDLN	LBDLDLN = (LBXTC/0.948 – LBDHDD/0.971 – (LBXTR/8.56 + (LBXTR * (LBXTC – LBDHDD))/2140 – LBXTR^2/16100) – 9.44), round 0 decimal places) for LBXTR less than 800 mg/dL, and missing for LBXTR GE 800 mg/dL. ^2 stands for power=2, or squared.
